  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_05535a53-7c26-4d81-b915-0547363eec02'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

<div id="review_775477488" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/775477488" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/775477488?book_show_action=true">Nov 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18758916-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=not-yet-released">not-yet-released</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer775477488" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8604772533828232764"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 stars!!</b><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433704946i/15133312.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>What. An. AWESOME. Ride!!! </b><br/><br/>Holy wow, I totally LOVED this book!! Dark and gritty, sweet and sexy, raw and shocking, and utterly addictive, with an unapologetic, badass Alpha male hero and unexpected twists that I never saw coming!! I couldn’t put it down from the moment I started it reading and I can’t wait for the next one!<br/><br/>TM Frazier writes some of the best dark romance out there. Her writing is strong and compelling. It keeps you on the edge of your se</span>
  <span id="freeText8604772533828232764" style="display:none"><b>::: FULL REVIEW NOW POSTED ::: 4.5 stars!!</b><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433704946i/15133312.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What. An. AWESOME. Ride!!! </b><br><br>Holy wow, I totally LOVED this book!! Dark and gritty, sweet and sexy, raw and shocking, and utterly addictive, with an unapologetic, badass Alpha male hero and unexpected twists that I never saw coming!! I couldn’t put it down from the moment I started it reading and I can’t wait for the next one!<br><br>TM Frazier writes some of the best dark romance out there. Her writing is strong and compelling. It keeps you on the edge of your seat and doesn’t hold back. Her characters hover in that mysterious and intriguing grey zone between good and bad and keep you constantly second guessing how you should feel about them. They’re incredibly complex and honestly, that’s what makes them so fascinating. And while her stories are raw and gritty, they always have a side of sweet and are woven with just enough depth and emotion to tug all your heart strings and really make you care. She’s definitely an auto-buy author for me!<br><br><blockquote>______________<br>Homeless. Hungry. Desperate.<br><br>Doe has no memories of who she is or where she comes from.<br><br>A notorious career criminal just released from prison, King is someone you don’t want to cross unless you’re prepared to pay him back in blood, sweat, sex or a combination of all three.<br><br>King’s future hangs in the balance. Doe’s is written in her past. When they come crashing together, they will have to learn that sometimes in order to hold on, you have to first let go.<br>______________</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"They call me King."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>King. Brantley King. Career criminal. Tattoo artist. Badass alpha. Fresh out of prison. -- <i>“This guy didn’t look like he hung with the wrong crowd. This guy was the wrong crowd.”</i> -- He grew up in merciless world, living on the edge. And a product of a brutal life, he was dark, dangerous, and totally untamed.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“So he’s not going to kill me?” I asked hopefully.<br>Didn’t say that… He’s not the most predictable guy, and he’s been away for a few years…”<br>“Years?… Where was he?”<br>“State.”<br>“College?”<br>“Prison.”<br>Prison made much more sense than college.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Doe was the complete opposite. Her past was a mystery to her -- after waking up in a garbage dump in a heap of her own blood with no memory of who she was or where she came from, the only thing she had left was a reflection in the mirror that even she didn't recognize. She wasn't cut for his world. Tiny, frail, but surprisingly bold and fiesty. Everything about him screamed danger to her, but even though he scared the hell out of her, I loved the way she still didn't take any of his shit...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>He expected me to cower.<br><br>He expected wrong.<br><br>“I don’t give a fuck who you are, asshole.” I seethed. “And you’re not as smart as you seem to think you are. Tell me something, who exactly was it who appointed you judge of all people?”<br><br>I thought my words would start an all out war but instead King didn’t look angrier, he only looked mildly amused. “Well you are partially right. Because when it comes to me and mine, I am the judge. I am the jury. And if need be, I am the motherfucking executioner.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>They got off to a rocky start. A girl like her had no place in his world and he wasn't about to start changing things. He had a single minded goal since getting out of prison (its a secret, you'll find out when you read) and would do anything he had to to get it. She was a detour he never expected. She brought out a whole other side of him. He wanted to own her, possess her, but slowly but surely, she began to steal his heart.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“King was smart, calculating, and cunning. Worst of all, he had the power to make my knees both tremble in fear and weak with desire. He was someone I had to stay away from, but according to him, that wasn’t about to happen."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I don't want to tell you too much more about the story because it's such a twisty journey (with shocking reveals that I never saw coming) that you should really just experience it for yourselves. Heads up though, there might be a trigger warning for some readers but the good guys do come in and save the day. This author really doesn't hold back and many of the events are dark and gritty. I keep coming back to those two words because they really are the best descriptors for the feeling of this story. But she writes that style like no one else. Her writing is just so strong and compelling that the pages flew by for me.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He’d told me that I was his before, that I belonged to him. But before that night, I hadn’t believed him.<br><br>It was what his body told me that took me by surprise and shook me to my very core.<br><br>He was mine."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Between the sexy hotness, the shocking reveals and plot twists, and surprisingly hilarious one-liners, this was an unputdownable book with strong underlying messages about the strength of friendship, the bonds of loyalty, love, and family, and also a reminder not to judge people on their outward appearances.<br><br>The ending had my heart in my throat -- huge reveals, huge twists (yes, plural!) -- and now I'm absolutely desperate to read the next book to see how it all ends. Admittedly, it's very rare for me to read a book with a cliffhanger so I pick and choose the ones I read very carefully. This was definitely one worth reading to me and I'm so glad I'm so glad that I gave it a shot, I loved the whole story start to finish, and I can't wait for the sequel to see where the whole story goes! Especially with that last twist. <i> Oh my!! </i><br><br>This is the first book in a 2-book series. The sequel Tyrant will be out in August. I'm personally glad I read this now though and didn't wait!<br><br>Fans of dark, gritty stories, with badass Alpha male heroes are sure to fall in love with King!!<br><br><b>Rating: 4.5 stars. Contemporary Adult dark romance.</b><br>Release day: June 15, 2015. <br><br>_______________________________________<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com/subscribe/" rel="nofollow noopener">Subscribe by email</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8604772533828232764" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13063118227456956660"><b>5 stars!!!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/fb195d79-2345-426d-8ec8-ab4034b0be79_zpsfzicvt9z.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433841835i/15149226.jpg' alt=' photo fb195d79-2345-426d-8ec8-ab4034b0be79_zpsfzicvt9z.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Love is what you would do for the other person, not what you do in general.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b>  When I read T.M. Frazier’s first book, <i>The Dark Light of Day</i>, in 2013 and I was hooked. I love this author’s writing style, the way she can write so much beauty among all the ugly content she writes and the feelings her books evoke. I feel like I have been waiting for the longest time for her second full length novel, <i>King</i>- but let me tell you guys something… KING was worth the wait! <br/><br/>Our stor</span>
  <span id="freeText13063118227456956660" style="display:none"><b>5 stars!!!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/fb195d79-2345-426d-8ec8-ab4034b0be79_zpsfzicvt9z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433841835i/15149226.jpg" alt=" photo fb195d79-2345-426d-8ec8-ab4034b0be79_zpsfzicvt9z.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Love is what you would do for the other person, not what you do in general.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b>  When I read T.M. Frazier’s first book, <i>The Dark Light of Day</i>, in 2013 and I was hooked. I love this author’s writing style, the way she can write so much beauty among all the ugly content she writes and the feelings her books evoke. I feel like I have been waiting for the longest time for her second full length novel, <i>King</i>- but let me tell you guys something… KING was worth the wait! <br><br>Our story starts with a young Doe. A girl with no memories. She doesn’t have anywhere to go, doesn’t know who she is and is alone in the world. <br><i>
  <blockquote>I don’t know where I came from.<br>I don’t know how hold I am<br>I don’t know my real name.</blockquote>
</i> <br>Some way or another, she finds King. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/2afc7378-ce7c-49ec-b172-3b43ca99693e_zpsymlj529y.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433841835i/15149227.jpg" alt=" photo 2afc7378-ce7c-49ec-b172-3b43ca99693e_zpsymlj529y.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Brantley King is a tattoo artist fresh out of prison. He is a criminal and has been for a long time. He and his partner, Preppy, have a business. They started from the very bottom when they were young but they were determined to make it. Now they’re on the top. They do what they want when they want to do it, no questions asked. When King first sees Doe, he doesn’t know what to think. He feels something for this girl. She makes him feel something different. <br><i>
  <blockquote>“Why did you come back for me?”<br><br> “Because you’re mine.”</blockquote>
</i><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/47f68539-755b-4519-937c-59d81774c174_zpsf5g3jusi.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433841835i/15149228.jpg" alt=" photo 47f68539-755b-4519-937c-59d81774c174_zpsf5g3jusi.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is so much I want to say about this story- SO MUCH! But at the risk of spoiling something (trust me, this is one you don’t want spoiled) I’ll just talk about the characters and all the things I loved. <br><br>First there was Doe. This girl was lost. She was frightened. But she was so strong. She was willing to do what it took to survive at all costs. And I love that as scary as King could be, she stood up to him. She didn’t cower and take his crap. King is a tough nut to crack. There are so many sides to this man. You see him as a ‘bad guy’ at first, but he is definitely not all bad. Doe brings out an eternity different guy. I love the connection they share and their chemistry is off the charts! Also, the more you hear about King’s past and what’s really going on in his life, the more you’ll feel for this powerful yet broken man. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/f03148b6-666f-4e1c-8a8b-95587b05a58c_zpsdqfqemlg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433841835i/15149229.jpg" alt=" photo f03148b6-666f-4e1c-8a8b-95587b05a58c_zpsdqfqemlg.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>As much as I loved the main characters, there are two secondary characters that were also fantastic. Preppy and Bear. Preppy is one of those guys that will make you laugh out loud in every part he’s in. He has the foulest mouth and you never know what he’s going to say. He’s a true friend to King and Doe in every sense of the word. Then there is Bear who is a biker and also a friend of King and Preppy’s. I think a Bear book would be pretty great. I’d love to know more about him. <br><br>Now lets get to what you all really want to hear about… that ending! Wow. That last 15% not only gutted me, but shocked me. I love getting those twists thrown into books that I didn’t see coming. And I for real did not see that coming! That cliffhanger makes me desperate for the next book. August can’t come soon enough! <br><br>If you are a fan of dark romances, read this book. If you want to be captivated by fantastic writing, read this book. If you like the raw and gritty, read this book. If you love twists and turns in your stories, read this book. I guess when it comes down to it, I would tell all my fellow readers to <b>read this book!</b> I loved it from start to finish and it’s one I highly recommend. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20Reviews%207/7ccc9960-7bb3-4a07-a3b7-409f38b11a3c_zpsqiaujp9x.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433841835i/15149230.jpg" alt=" photo 7ccc9960-7bb3-4a07-a3b7-409f38b11a3c_zpsqiaujp9x.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13063118227456956660" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1297326931" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1297326931" />
    <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance"><img alt="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1376622739p2/5498948.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1297326931?book_show_action=true">Jun 02, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾" href="/user/show/5498948-lana-dg-romance">Lana ❇✾DG Romance❇✾</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=auto-buy-authors">auto-buy-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=cliffhanger">cliffhanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=erotic">erotic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=tissues-needed">tissues-needed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=favorite-alpha-hero">favorite-alpha-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5498948-lana-dg-romance?shelf=dark-read">dark-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1297326931" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15944983394806313991"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br/><img src='https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433562890r/15113613.jpg?v=1433562893760' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png' width='50' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>I've found myself again in the haunted eyes of a girl who was just as lost as I was.<br/>Or maybe, we didn't find each other at all.<br/>Maybe, we just decided to be lost together.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404536077ra/10253583.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I've been a huge fan on this author ever since I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18278129.The_Dark_Light_of_Day__The_Dark_Light_of_Day___1_' title='The Dark Light of Day (The Dark Light of Day, #1) by T.M. Frazier' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Dark Light of Day</a>. So when I saw that she was coming out with this book and I read that synopsis? Suffice it to say I was willing to part with an ovary to finally get my hands on this beauty. Waiting the extra time since the original release date has </span>
  <span id="freeText15944983394806313991" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars</b><br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433562890r/15113613.jpg?v=1433562893760" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I've found myself again in the haunted eyes of a girl who was just as lost as I was.<br>Or maybe, we didn't find each other at all.<br>Maybe, we just decided to be lost together.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1404536077ra/10253583.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I've been a huge fan on this author ever since I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18278129.The_Dark_Light_of_Day__The_Dark_Light_of_Day___1_" title="The Dark Light of Day (The Dark Light of Day, #1) by T.M. Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">The Dark Light of Day</a>. So when I saw that she was coming out with this book and I read that synopsis? Suffice it to say I was willing to part with an ovary to finally get my hands on this beauty. Waiting the extra time since the original release date has been absolute torture, but then T.M. announced it won't be a standalone. Suffice it to say I was ready to stab someone in an ovary at that point. I don't do well with numerous books for same characters. I get bored, find the story stretched out, get tired of the same characters, and to be quite honest most often than not I find the story could have easily been resolved in one book. But I shouldn't have doubted this author because she not only brought it with this book, she <b>brought</b> it. It is definitely not a story that was meant for a standalone and I can understand completely why it's split into two parts. As a matter of fact, it made the story that much better. Yeah. I just said that. I'll give you a moment to get over your shock. Moving on...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">This guy didn't look like he hung with the wrong crowd. This guy was the wrong crowd.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>King is the very epitome of a bad boy. A criminal that goes after what he wants with a lethal determination, he's not someone you want on your bad side. Growing up with an alcoholic mother hasn't given him much, he was forced to take it. Alongside with his best friend, Preppy, they've built an impressive reputation. Now recently out of a stint in maximum security prison, King wants to drown himself in pussy and alcohol when <i>she</i> stumbles right into his path.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I don't know where I came from.<br>I don't know how old I am.<br>I don't know my real name.<br>All I had in the world was reflected back at me in the bathroom mirror of that gas station, and I had no fucking clue who she was.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433882360ra/15153965.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Doe woke up in a hospital with absolutely no recollection of how she got there or who she is. She doesn't even know her name, simply goes by Doe as in <i>Jane Doe</i>. Forced to fend for herself on the streets, starving and desperate she's willing to do anything for a hot meal and a roof to sleep under...even give her body to a biker in exchange for protection. But when the biker she sets her eyes on sends her to his friend instead, she stumbles right into King's path. She may look like she's been through hell, but something about her ignites King and he knows that he needs to have her.<br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433562891r/15113614.jpg?v=1433562893876" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>What takes place then is sexual tension of unbearable proportions. The push and pull between them is a burn that hurt so good. While the chemistry between them is instant, it's not something they either of them gives into right away.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Pup, do you want to know how it is that I know you weren't dreaming about me when you were not he verge of coming in your sleep?"<br>"Yes," I whispered.<br>"Cause, baby, if it were me you were dreaming about, you'd been screaming a fuck of a lot louder than that," King growled.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414374318ra/11646167.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I have to admit, I wasn't sure about the first half of this book. Besides King's criminal activity, there really wasn't much grit or darkness to it. There was quite a bit of character and story development though. While Doe has no idea who she is and where she came from, King does. But he's not about to let her know because selfishly he wants her for himself even though he gets to be an unbearable asshole about it.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Why don't you just gut me and get it over with? Do whatever it is you want to do to me. Hit me. Fuck me. Fucking KILL me. Just. Stop. HURTING. Me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved that even though Doe was homeless and thrown into a world she knew nothing about, she still had a backbone. Girl had some sass to her and she definitely gave as good as she got and slowly you get to see the big bad King fall more and more...<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">Against my better judgement, I'd brought her back to my house. I fed her. I bathed her. I put her to bed, and she didn't fight me off when I climbed in beside her and held her close while she cried herself to sleep. She was here against her will and I was one fucked up motherfucker.<br>Because I'd never been happier.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Luckily he never loses his edge either. While his feelings for Doe turn into something that's beyond simple lust, he's still a criminal and he's certainly not looking to change his ways. And the man was pure sex on a stick.<br><img src="https://s3.amazonaws.com/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433562891r/15113615.jpg?v=1433562893879" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I think what I loved the most is that way that T.M. Frazier managed to give him this element of vulnerability without taking away from his edge. He may not be perfect, but every now and then you get the glimpse inside the heart of a man that's been through hell.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380397315i/766520.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">I've been in a maximum security prison. I've been around the worst of the worst. I've had to sleep with one eye open, thinking my next breath could be my last."<br>"Why are you telling me all this?"<br>"Because I want you to know that none of those motherfuckers ever scared me as much as you do."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The author gives you a brilliant story that lulls you into a false sense of security because right around the 85% she will rip the rug out from right under your feet. Mother fucker of feels but the woman is a pure sadist because when she goes for the feels she does it like a damn pitbull. She will grip you by the heart and rip that fucker right out of your chest...then stomp on it for good measure...laughing while she does it.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433883494ra/15154069.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nothing and I mean NOTHING will prepare you for what happens. It's filled with so many twists and turns that your head will spin and your heart will bleed. And then she hits you with that cliffhanger. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432074327ra/14897412.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So at this point in time I'm pretty much willing to part with an ovary AND a kidney just to get my hands on the second book noooooooow.<br><br>This is part 1 of a 2 book series and I'm thrilled that the third book will be Bear because who doesn't love a hot ass biker? King was very much worth the wait and I can definitely tell you that T.M. definitely hasn't lost her touch. Read it and see exactly what I'm talking about.<br><br><i>ARC courtesy of author in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br><b>For more reviews visit<br><a href="http://dirtygirlromance.com" target="blogspot" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1436477285i/15465455._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="15944983394806313991" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_830412253" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/830412253" />
    <a title="Pam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13865261-pam"><img alt="Pam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374039144p2/13865261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/830412253?book_show_action=true">Jan 21, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pam" href="/user/show/13865261-pam">Pam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=5">5</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=darkerside-mindfuckery">darkerside-mindfuckery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=suspense-chills-n-thrills">suspense-chills-n-thrills</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=steamy-hawt">steamy-hawt</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=tats-n-piercings">tats-n-piercings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=fucked-up-n-broken">fucked-up-n-broken</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13865261-pam?shelf=sixty-first-reads">sixty-first-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer830412253" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3982947612134387776"><i>5 Desperate people. Desperate things. stars</i><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Stop being alive, and start living.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434435622i/15220866._SY540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/> <br/><b>Holy Fucking Hell</b> ...seriously I have no clue how I am going to explain myself when I can't even begin to tell you (without spoiling of course) what this book did to me or how it <i>made</i> me feel! Because I have to tell you, I <i>felt </i><u>every damn thing</u>. I'm going to keep this short, because honestly the only thing you need to know going in, is KING is the ultimate bad guy with the biggest heart for those he love</span>
  <span id="freeText3982947612134387776" style="display:none"><i>5 Desperate people. Desperate things. stars</i><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Stop being alive, and start living.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434435622i/15220866._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br><b>Holy Fucking Hell</b> ...seriously I have no clue how I am going to explain myself when I can't even begin to tell you (without spoiling of course) what this book did to me or how it <i>made</i> me feel! Because I have to tell you, I <i>felt </i><u>every damn thing</u>. I'm going to keep this short, because honestly the only thing you need to know going in, is KING is the ultimate bad guy with the biggest heart for those he loves. <br><br>Imagine waking up hurt, with no memories, no name and the sad, sad truth of no one looking for you. That is the reality of Doe, as in Jane Doe, she was thrown into the world with no where to go, no food and no protection. She is taken in by a crack addict hooker, who shares with her the secret of surviving the streets... attach yourself to a biker for a warm bed, food and protection, all you have to is keep him happy by any means necessary. But what sounds like a good plan in theory, doesn't seem so so easy to do once faced with the reality, especially when said biker practically gives you away as a welcome home gift for King, the bad ass career criminal who just got out of prison. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I am the judge. I am the jury. And if need be, I am the motherfucking executioner.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434435622i/15220867._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Doe is King's salvation and personal hell, she doesn't know it yet but she holds so much power over King more than anyone else in the world... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434435622i/15220868._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fate may have brought them together, but it will be Karma that will make them pay...all King knows is that no one crosses him, especially without paying him back in sweat, pu$$y or <i>blood.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434435622i/15220869.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>KING</b> is one intense, non-stop roller coaster ride of emotions. This story is told from both King's and Doe's point of view, which I absolutely loved because I lived each moment with them. How could I not feel for Doe, confused and desperate, there is no telling what anyone is capable of, luckily she is made from much stronger cloth than most and cared for the "Her" she was while doing the best for the "Her" she is. King lived up to every expectation I had conjured up for him, big and bad, totally naughty and a big 'ol softy when it matters most. I do have to bring one more character into the mix, Preppy, god love him and his foul mouth, crazy ass smile and adorable bad ass bow ties. <br><br>This book strung me along effortlessly with the flow and ease of how their story is told. It all clicked into place, one event after another, the new one more intense than the past! I have to admit, going in knowing this was not a stand alone, I braced long before when it was needed, but you can't blame me for wanting to protect my emotions, and while I was smart to brace because right till the very end, my heart dropped, then it soared, giving me new hope. It is with that new found hope that I will be able to survive until their story continues on, because now the possibilities are endless and the reward will be so much sweeter especially when King kick's some ass along the way. <br><br>Amazing job and recommended read for sure!<br><br><i>ARC kindly provided by the author, in exchange for an honest review.</i><br> <br>***Quotes above are taken from the ARC version of the book and may differ upon publication.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3982947612134387776" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_831259044" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/831259044" />
    <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog"><img alt="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518242765p2/14302918.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/831259044?book_show_action=true">Jan 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog" href="/user/show/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog">Patty ~ Wrapped Up In Reading Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=unbearable-angst">unbearable-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=top-fantasy-boyfriends">top-fantasy-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=dark-reads">dark-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14302918-patty-wrapped-up-in-reading-book-blog?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer831259044" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16441046788138818392"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br/>{BR with Mel, Sharon, Tiff, Jen, and Tera}<br/><br/><br/><b> King filled me so completely. Not just my body. My heart. My soul. My life. I didn't give a shit if I ever got my memory back. Because with King, I knew exactly who I was.</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/06b6cfb7698a8a8d8ca4bddc9ac63b26_zps9kvlife6.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434689661i/15253470._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 06b6cfb7698a8a8d8ca4bddc9ac63b26_zps9kvlife6.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Brantley King is an ex con just released from prison after serving a three year sentence. He has led a shitty life since childhood. When he was twelve, he saved a kid who was being beaten in the playground by the school bully and the two form a fast friendship t</span>
  <span id="freeText16441046788138818392" style="display:none"><b>*****FIVE STARS*****</b><br>{BR with Mel, Sharon, Tiff, Jen, and Tera}<br><br><br><b> King filled me so completely. Not just my body. My heart. My soul. My life. I didn't give a shit if I ever got my memory back. Because with King, I knew exactly who I was.</b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/06b6cfb7698a8a8d8ca4bddc9ac63b26_zps9kvlife6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434689661i/15253470._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 06b6cfb7698a8a8d8ca4bddc9ac63b26_zps9kvlife6.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>Brantley King is an ex con just released from prison after serving a three year sentence. He has led a shitty life since childhood. When he was twelve, he saved a kid who was being beaten in the playground by the school bully and the two form a fast friendship that will end up turning them into the only family they've ever known. "Preppy" comes up with a plan to sell pot so that the two can make money and eventually buy their own home. He's definitely an odd character that marches to the beat of his own drum but you'll see that it's quite impossible not to fall in love with the guy.<br><br><br><br>On King's first night home from prison, Preppy and his other friend, Bear, throw him a welcome home party. Doe, a pretty young girl, ends up going to this party with her friend who is a crack whore. Doe has amnesia and doesn't remember her identity nor her past. She ends up on the streets and befriends this hooker. She's at this party because her friend tells her she can hook up with a biker from the local MC, who will more than likely take her in and give her food and shelter. What she gets instead is held captive as King's property due to a huge misunderstanding. This may sound horrible, but actually I wouldn't mind being in Doe's shoes because King is all kinds of alpha hotness!!<br><br><br><br>He's completely turned on by Doe and intrigued as well. Doe feels a pull towards King, but is fighting it because she doesn't want to do anything that will cause any turmoil to her life if she ever does regain her memory.<br><br><br><br>This is not a "Hearts &amp; Flowers" romance, and King is not the knight in shining armor, coming to rescue the damsel in distress. He's done bad things. He's also never felt anything for a woman until he meets Doe. I knew going in that this would be a dark and gritty read! I've read <b>"The Dark Light of Day"</b>, and absolutely <b>LOVED</b> that book!! Believe me when I say that this book is no where near as dark as her previous one. T.M Frazier writes so well that she evokes all kinds of emotions from you. I was reading this on the train to NYC and could hardly sit still in my seat. I was cringing and pulling my hair!!!<br><br><br><br><br>There are some really painful scenes in this one and definitely a devastating event. I believe that is why some people rated it so low. But I know this author's style and she will never go the predictable route. She likes to turn shit upside down and throw things at you that you never saw coming. And that's why I love this author and couldn't see rating this anything less than <b>FIVE STARS</b>!!!!!<br><br><br><br>It ends on an incredible cliffy, but the next book comes out in August. So that's not too long of a wait!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16441046788138818392" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1784587263" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1784587263" />
    <a title="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog"><img alt="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471840369p2/37057510.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1784587263?book_show_action=true">Oct 30, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥" href="/user/show/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog">Jessica ❥Chatterbooks Book Blog❥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37057510-jessica-chatterbooks-book-blog?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1784587263" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3224719847235864458">4.5 stars<br/><br/>What a story! I stayed up all night long reading this, because I just couldn't put it down. Seriously, I read the last few chapters with only one eye open! lol When I got to the end, I was speechless. Well, almost speechless....I did utter the words "holy shit." I had so many conflicting emotions. I literally couldn't isolate any of them enough to know exactly how I felt. After some much needed sleep, I have to say I barely have a grip now. Forgive me if my review is a little all over t</span>
  <span id="freeText3224719847235864458" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />What a story! I stayed up all night long reading this, because I just couldn't put it down. Seriously, I read the last few chapters with only one eye open! lol When I got to the end, I was speechless. Well, almost speechless....I did utter the words "holy shit." I had so many conflicting emotions. I literally couldn't isolate any of them enough to know exactly how I felt. After some much needed sleep, I have to say I barely have a grip now. Forgive me if my review is a little all over the place.<br /><br />I'm not going to write a summary for this, because at this point I think everybody and their grandma knows what this is about. I feel like I'm the last person on the planet to read this series. Seeing everyone's excitement for the new book that just came out about Preppy gave me the push I needed to finally pick this one up.<br /><br />King is the first book I have ever read by T.M. Frazier. I see many more in my future, because this book was amazing! It was not perfect by any means, but it made me FEEL! I felt so many emotions while reading this that I could barely keep up with them all. It made laugh and even made me cry. I don't cry often while reading, so that's really saying something. T. M. Frazier, you ripped my heart out!! Why??!! Did that really have to happen??!! <br /><br />From the very first chapter, I suspected that I was going to love this book. King and Preppy's first meeting is one I'm sure I'll always remember. Getting just those few flashbacks from their childhood brought more depth to both their character and their relationship. I adored the friendship and brotherhood between these two, not to mention, the dynamic between King, Preppy, and Doe. The three of them together always left me with a smile on my face.<br /><br />Doe and King are an odd couple brought about by awful circumstances, but I was rooting for them almost the whole time (minus the couple of times I wanted to murder King for being a big, fat, jerkface.) :) The sexual tension between these two is palpable from the first time they lay eyes on each other. When they finally get together, it is hot! When they weren't confusing the hell out of each other or pushing each other away, they brought out the best in each other. Doe brought out the softer, kinder, more caring side of King, and he brought out the bolder, braver, more daring side of her. <br /><br />The characters in this story were complex, flawed, and messed up individuals. King, Preppy, and Bear are criminals and have been since they were kids. That's not all there is to them though, and that's what makes them endearing to the reader. They may be bad men, but they don't always do bad things. They are capable of love, friendship, selflessness, and loyalty. For most of the story, Doe doesn't know who she is, and we have no back story for her. She appears sweet and innocent, but by the end of the book we see that she is probably a little different than what we thought. <br /><br />The character that drove me crazy throughout the whole story was King. I loved him, I hated him, I was confused, I wanted to stab him, I hated him, I love him again, and then I wanted to hug him while I beat him in the face! He would do awful things, but then he would do something like go and take care of a dying old woman. His changing moods and contradictory actions gave me whiplash. This man was something else! In the end, despite all his imperfections, I couldn't help but want the best for him.<br /><br />I can't conclude this review without talking a little more about my favorite character, Preppy. I loved Preppy from his first bloody smile. A walking contradiction, with his bow ties and tattoos, he lit up the page everytime he appeared. He was dealt a shitty hand in life, but he didn't let that keep him down. Preppy always made the best out of everything. Amazingly odd, fun, light hearted, messed up and perverted, foul mouthed and endearing; he was an incredible character to read about.<br /><br />That cliffhanger was BRUTAL! Thank God, I already have the next 3 books waiting for me on my kindle. If I didn't, I would have been really angry. lol If there is anyone else out there left in the world that hasn't read this book, what are you waiting for?? Do it, right now!! :D</span>
  <a data-text-id="3224719847235864458" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2h87m94" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271123.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqovg3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271124.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b> “Brantley King"</b><i> was 12 years old when he met his best friend <b>“Samuel Clearwater” aka “Preppy”</b> who was only 11 yrs old himself. They both wanted out of their miserable family they were given. King’s mom was a drug junkie and he basically had to care for himself until he decided to run away from it. Preppy’s step father was an absolute ass hole who abused Preppy so bad I wanted to kill him myself. Now the boys are grown man who grew up making their own rules and living by their own laws doing illegal things to survive. King was 27 yrs old and Pretty 26 now. They both killed if it was necessary and started selling drugs and other illegal things at young age in order to make money and make their “dreams” come true. At a young age they thought they were on top of the world, parting a lot and enjoying what life they were making together. King was great with art and he started doing tattoos from his house practicing on himself, Preppy and Bear (a friend they met at young age at school).</i> <br><br><p>
  <b>
    <i>"Well you are partially right. Because when it comes to me and mine, I am the judge. I am the jury. And if need be, I am the motherfucking executioner." King</i>
  </b>
</p><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2199lx5" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434856941i/15271908._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqovg3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271124.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Doe” aka “PUP” or “Ray”</b><i>, a seventeen year old girl lost with no memory, living in group homes or on the streets; founds Nikki, someone who she thought could helped her. After having an accident and losing her memory, Doe now had no one and took shelter with Nikki. However her new friend was a junkie and didn’t care about anything else other than her next fix. Doe had no recollection of her previews life, and there was no missing person report matching her description; that left her lonely with nothing and no one. Nikki takes her to a party and the goal was for Doe to attempt to sell herself for protection and shelter to one of the MC bikers. What she didn’t know was that this wasn’t just any party it was a “Welcome Party” for King. He had just being release from prison after being incarcerated for three years. She hadn’t eaten for days so she was bound to do whatever it takes to survive even if that meant selling her body. </i> <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=jv2lg2" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434856941i/15271909._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><p>
  <b>
    <i>"Desperate people. Desperate things." Doe</i>
  </b>
</p><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=24cwjs4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271125.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqovg3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271124.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“Bear”</b><i> a hot biker who is best friends with King and Preppy; and the Vice president for his father’s MC club the “Beach Bastards”. He meets Doe first at the party and wants her for himself but he wanted to give his best friend a welcome back gift and sends her over to KING. This changed the story entirely, Doe and King didn’t realized that there was going to be a magnetic chemistry between the two that will pull them together and change their lives forever. <br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2i0ds7q" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434856941i/15271910._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqovg3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271124.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>King</b><i> takes</i><b> Doe</b><i> in after finding out who she was and he wanted to keep her for his own benefit. However he decides to keep the secret to himself. Preppy saw the connection between these two and wanted to push King’s buttons so he would step up and claim Doe and hopefully be happy. He was amazing and funny, I loved him so much. Preppy becomes good friends with Doe in the little time she came to live with them. He would make her pancakes every day and made her eat, she loved him for it. He wanted to take her out on a date as a friend but I think, he wanted to see King’s reaction and pushed him so it worked. King ended up taking her on his very first date; he never did dates so this was his first. And oh boy it was everything a first date should be; he was amazing he took her to the carnival “Neon lights, carnival music, corn dog and cotton candy stands” just perfect. They had this amazing HOT kiss on the Ferris Wheel it was super cute for KING really. He gave her the first tattoo she’s ever had and it was just perfect and beautiful.</i> <br><br></i><p>
  <b>
    <i> “As King branded my skin, I embraced the girl whose life was just beginning. I embraced life. My life. King filled me so completely. Not just my body. My heart. My soul. My life. I didn’t give a shit if I ever got my memory back. Because with King, I knew exactly who I was. I was his.” Doe</i>
  </b>
</p><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=20ur952" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271126.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>He wanted to stop the feelings he was getting for her so he pushed her away purposely trying to make out with someone else when they got back from their date. I was a so upset omg…I was beyond angry at him. However, the angry sex helped me calmed down a bit and it up for it lol. He ended up claiming her and she opened up to him and they both gave into each other.</i> <br><br><p>
  <b>
    <i> “We get this one life. One. As of right this fucking second, I’m no longer going to spend it doing anything other than what I want to do. I don’t want to grow old and look back and realize that I may have had a life, but I forgot to live it.” King</i>
  </b>
</p><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=neykio" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851387ra/15271127.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=kaqwls" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851629ra/15271144.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqovg3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271124.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>The events after they finally became a couple shred me to pieces. He confessed his dark secrets to her but still keep the secret of who she really was to himself but I melted for him at that point. Something horrible and unexpected also happens right at 86% of the book that I can’t even bring myself to write because I don’t want to give any spoilers. I was so broken and a complete mess from then up until the end. The ending was completely unexpected and now I have more questions than ever. I wish book two was already out because this waiting is going to kill me. However, I did read the epilogue for book two I had to, like there was no way this book could possibly end like this so it gave me a little hope and now to count down the days for book two. This was my very first book by this author and I can assure you it will not be my last. I am looking forward to more of her writing.</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=x5cz03" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434856941i/15271911._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqovg3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271124.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><p>
  <b>
    <i> “There was no doubt in my mind if something like soulmates did exist that Doe was mine…I think a part of me loved Doe from the first moment my eyes landed on hers. Haunted, beautiful, scared. I wanted her, body and soul.” King</i>
  </b>
</p><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=vr81og" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434902988ra/15276574.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><p>
  <b>
    <i> “King was a bad guy, but he was my bad guy. He was more than that. He was my world. My heart. These people may have known who I was before, but I knew who I was now, and the two versions of me were going to have to figure out how to merge before I uprooted what I had with King in search of something unknown.” Doe</i>
  </b>
</p><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=eqovg3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434851386ra/15271124.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>BR WITH MY SHHLUTS ~ WAR, LIZ AND NAWAL ~</i>
</b><br><br><b>Book Series Order:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25659331.King__King___1_" title="King (King, #1) by T.M. Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/759187876?book_show_action=true">Nov 07, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brandi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brandi" href="/user/show/5494655-brandi">Brandi</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5494655-brandi?shelf=top-tbr">top-tbr</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer759187876" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11888366042923345064"><br/>I was hoping after taking sometime to cool down, and reflect on the story, I would feel differently. I tried. Honest. I really did.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434570778ra/15239099.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But, I failed. I'm still upset :/ So I guess I'll be in the minority, because I just did not love this book. Maybe my expectations were too high. Idk. <br/><br/>Regardless, this was a fast paced read, with some interesting characters, in fact a few of those characters outshined our MCs. <br/><br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[To the character that made the story, <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434572625ra/15239389.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br/><br/> I struggled with King</span>
  <span id="freeText11888366042923345064" style="display:none"><br>I was hoping after taking sometime to cool down, and reflect on the story, I would feel differently. I tried. Honest. I really did.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434570778ra/15239099.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But, I failed. I'm still upset :/ So I guess I'll be in the minority, because I just did not love this book. Maybe my expectations were too high. Idk. <br><br>Regardless, this was a fast paced read, with some interesting characters, in fact a few of those characters outshined our MCs. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[To the character that made the story, <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434572625ra/15239389.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br> I struggled with King, honestly, he was a walking contradiction, he gave me whiplash and a headache. I enjoyed Doe, while she was a bit too forgiving at times. The storyline had potential, but occasionally felt choppy and OTT. Most of the drama seemed random and pointless. In the end I just felt disappointed. But maybe I'm bitter. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434571236ra/15239144.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_1302166784" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1302166784" />
    <a title="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26191846-shabby--bookbistroblog"><img alt="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1562639151p2/26191846.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1302166784?book_show_action=true">Jun 08, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shabby  -BookBistroBlog" href="/user/show/26191846-shabby--bookbistroblog">Shabby  -BookBistroBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Shabby  by: </span>
      t.m.frazier 
  </div>


    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1302166784" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer732555178581874288">What can I say about this amazing story. It's raw and gritty and angsty and angry and tumultuous and I Loved It . The rugged and scarred Brantley King with his best buddy Samuel 'Preppy' are the main characters , they meet 'Pup' and ......ughhh I don't wanna give away the story. <br/>It's a beautifully told story, t.m. makes us feel the hunger, pain, love, friendship, kinship, betrayal ,passion , all first hand . <br/>Write the next book faster TM , I'm dying here !</span>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1288194833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15046925130326754898"><a href='http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img alt='description' height='90' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427987214i/14347114.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>**FULL REVIEW POSTED**</b><br/><br/><b>Rating : 4.5 ‘Mofo’s’ Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433827260i/15147921._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='570' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>My Views :</b> I’m shaken right now; as if my mind just experienced a <b> hurricane. </b> <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422737786ra/13540246.gif' width='40' height='40' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> Seriously Folks, if there is one book that should be on your 2015 TBR, it’s KING by T.M.Frazier. <b> She made me smile, laugh, cry and wail and scream<img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433787481ra/15142670.gif' width='40' height='40' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> and speechless </b>. And MoFos August 17th??? Are you serious??? Honestly that climax, denouement and ending made my heart pump and palpitate. Thanks for the prologue of Tyrant but I need that fucking book more than my next</span>
  <span id="freeText15046925130326754898" style="display:none"><a href="http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="90" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427987214i/14347114.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>**FULL REVIEW POSTED**</b><br><br><b>Rating : 4.5 ‘Mofo’s’ Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433827260i/15147921._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="570" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>My Views :</b> I’m shaken right now; as if my mind just experienced a <b> hurricane. </b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422737786ra/13540246.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> Seriously Folks, if there is one book that should be on your 2015 TBR, it’s KING by T.M.Frazier. <b> She made me smile, laugh, cry and wail and scream<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433787481ra/15142670.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> and speechless </b>. And MoFos August 17th??? Are you serious??? Honestly that climax, denouement and ending made my heart pump and palpitate. Thanks for the prologue of Tyrant but I need that fucking book more than my next breath!!!<br><br><b>Style of writing :</b> Just what I needed. That was the extent of her writing. That woman seriously kicked ass with this one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433763725i/15139494._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Characters :</b> King was everything and more that I expect my bad boys to be. <b> He was sexy as Fuck and my God that man can make your panties do catwalk out of the room. </b> I more than drooled over him; <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433787481ra/15142671.gif" width="40" height="45" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> typical alpha and cocky attitude and lots of badass tattoos! That what a girl needs.<br><br>However, my favourite was Preppy! No ladies he’s not yours, I’m ready to stake my claim all <b>‘King Kong’ style…don’t cross me!!!</b> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433787481ra/15142672.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>This is my Preppy *Mwahhh*</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433827260i/15147922._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Doe is the cute heroine that you can’t help but feel pity for her. She totally won my heart and thank you to Miss Frazier for giving her heroine small tits (Gives me hope!!!) What! <b>Not all girls are well-endowed, some of us have mosquito bites!</b><br><br><b>Favourite Part :</b> From Preppy’s letter ‘Open Me Mofos’ till the end I read through blurred eyes and my shattered heart on the floor.<b> I was shocked, surprised, angry and pissed.</b> Yes, that was my idea of favourite! <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433787481ra/15142673.gif" width="40" height="40" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did not work?</b> Now the big question, why not 5 stars? Simply because there were many scenes which were predictable for me; however I am keeping those 5 stars for the second book.<br><br><b>Similar books? </b> Nope…None that I’ve read so far!<br><br><b>Recommended :</b> Are you kidding me!!! Definitely, <b>this book is priority right now.</b> However you have been warned “This book contains graphic violence, consensual and non-consensual sex, drug use, abuse, and other taboo subjects and adult subject matter.” And this is the first book in this series (will release July 15th), the second book ‘Tyrant’ will be out August 17th.<br><br><b>Click On The Color Splashes To Join Me ;)</b><br><a href="http://peekatmybookreview.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img alt="description" height="50" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1430844658i/14768810.png" width="50" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1318593537" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17553644351089230475">If you read one book this year, make it this one!!! Just finished this today and am still reeling in my thoughts about this one. Fantastic, just doesn't do it justice! So many emotions felt while reading this book! Perfectly written, flowed without any back tracking and to top it off, a story line that was deserving of a 5 star rating!!! Because Pancakes!!!</span>

          </span>

</a><br/><br/>EKkkkkkk I have waited and waited, stalked and stalked the author for this book, then when I saw it sitting in my trusty kindle I did the meanest Mr bean Dance ever invented!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Desperate people do desperat</i></b></span>
