</a><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=s6ndb9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433467756i/15100047._SY540_.png" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>TITLE:</b> King<br><b>SERIES:</b> (King #1)<br><b>AUTHOR:</b> T.M.Frazier<br><b>GENRE:</b> Contemporary Romance | New Adult<br><b>EXPECTED PUBLICATION:</b> June 15th, 2015<br><b>MY RATING: 5 STARS</b><br><br><b>༺**Complimentary Copy**༺</b> Provided by the Author in exchange for an Honest Review..Thank you!!<br><br><b>KING</b> is about Murder, Loss, Redemption, and LOVE<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=14kd30z" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433470571i/15100257._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>EKkkkkkk I have waited and waited, stalked and stalked the author for this book, then when I saw it sitting in my trusty kindle I did the meanest Mr bean Dance ever invented!!<br><br><b>
  <i>Desperate people do desperate things</i>
</b><br><br>Whoa this book had my mind in a tale spin, I raged, I laughed, I raged some more, KING in the beginning came across like a hardened alpha male kidnapper asshole, then slowly you see another softer side appear, even though I've finished this I still don't really know what made KING tick..I crazy loved this book, everything KING was done in one gear - fast..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2ev9ea0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433475491i/15100709._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The book starts off with KING just being released from his stint in prison, a welcome home party is under way, he's just finished tattooing a female, flips her over and is balls deep, when he's interrupted by a young female observing from the doorway which gives KING the much needed release, DOE is at the party with her street friend Nikki in the hopes of someone taking her under his wing and he gives her somewhere safe to lay her head and food in her undernourished body..Things take a turn for the worse when Nikki steals 6 grand from KING..He's out for vengeance..<br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=igkp4x" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433478890i/15100878._SX540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>DOE ~</b><i>If you took the scary out of the equation, <b>King</b> was drop dead gorgeous. His eyes were so dark green they almost looked black. His lips were full and slightly pink. He was the most terrifyingly beautiful thing I'd ever laid eyes on.</i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=bdmwxk" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433476465i/15100758._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>My Life. King filled me so completely. No just my body. My heart. My soul. My life. I didn't give a shit if I ever got my memory back. Because with King, I knew exactly who I was. I was his.</b>
</i><br><br>We got a glimpse of KING in "Dark Needs" and what his speciality was this book hopefully will delve deeper into what makes KING tick, what made him into the man he is today..<br><br><i>"You may be pretty, pup, and those eyes of yours get my cock hard, but you're all skin and bones. Besides, I don't fuck junkies." </i><br><br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=vnox2p" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433479183i/15100892._SY540_.jpg" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> In all the time I'd been living on the streets, I've had some close calls, some serious gut check moments. I've seen things that have made my skin crawl and my heart race. I was very familiar with feeling afraid.  Fear had nothing on King.</i><br><br><b>KING ~</b> GOOGLE IMAGE SEARCH <i>
  <b> That's all it took to find out who Doe really was, I wished I'd never done the search. I wished I'd never known who she really was.</b>

<span id="freeTextContainer14756814470495810355">Re-read note: I savored it the second time around. I think I saw King with a clearer perspective. He's raw, yes, but there was also this sweetness to him in subtle ways I didn't appreciate as much the first go.<br/><br/>First of all... Darn it, King! Why'd you have to go and do that for!?? It was going so well :( I get it, dammit, but I don't like it. <br/><br/>Now other thoughts: King is the bad boy asshole women flock to. He's raw. He's unapologetic.   <span id="freeText14756814470495810355" style="display:none">Re-read note: I savored it the second time around. I think I saw King with a clearer perspective. He's raw, yes, but there was also this sweetness to him in subtle ways I didn't appreciate as much the first go.<br /><br />First of all... Darn it, King! Why'd you have to go and do that for!?? It was going so well :( I get it, dammit, but I don't like it. <br /><br />Now other thoughts: King is the bad boy asshole women flock to. He's raw. He's unapologetic. He had this idgaf attitude you can't help but be drawn to. Little miss Doe is no exception. Even if it takes her a little longer to realize it. She's in a very difficult situation and by being in the wrong place, wrong time, things went from bad to FUBAR. She doesn't know who she is and has survived on the streets. She has finally reached her limit. This story touches on some pretty difficult subjects and I don't think it molds itself to what is conventionally considered right but what is right for who the characters are at the time. It's got some very dynamic and complex characters that have some flaws the size of Texas but you still can't help but get attached. Much to my dismay, it's a cliffy that I must finish right away but it does hook you quite well. I will be jumping on part two next for sure. Why the heck didn't I read this sooner? Lol Safety: H starts off story having sex with OW. None after that despite him trying to make h believe otherwise. Book contains rape and abuse. No OM, at least with consent. No sharing. Neither are Vs. There is pushing away.</span>

<div id="review_1279167763" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1279167763" />
    <a title="Jasmine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine"><img alt="Jasmine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1406624675p2/31339793.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1279167763?book_show_action=true">May 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jasmine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jasmine" href="/user/show/31339793-jasmine">Jasmine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=give-me-that-alpha-male">give-me-that-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=i-love-me-some-angst-drama">i-love-me-some-angst-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=top-2015-reads">top-2015-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=arc-reads">arc-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=freakin-cliffies">freakin-cliffies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=mystery-suspense">mystery-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/31339793-jasmine?shelf=motha-whiplash-emotions">motha-whiplash-emotions</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1279167763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12309734312080529999"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433603055i/15118815.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"If you fuck with me and what's mine, then yes, I am the judge. I am the jury. And sometimes when the situation calls for it, I am the motherfucking executioner."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Mark your calenders everyone. June 15 is the day to live by because embrace yourselves for the awesomeness that is <u>King</u>. Pick up this book, read it, devour it and when you're done freaking out over that ending, let's all give each other mental support to make it through the next. Okay? Okay moving on.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Brantley King</b> is a</span>
  <span id="freeText12309734312080529999" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS! ★★★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433603055i/15118815.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"If you fuck with me and what's mine, then yes, I am the judge. I am the jury. And sometimes when the situation calls for it, I am the motherfucking executioner."</i>
</b><br><br>Mark your calenders everyone. June 15 is the day to live by because embrace yourselves for the awesomeness that is <u>King</u>. Pick up this book, read it, devour it and when you're done freaking out over that ending, let's all give each other mental support to make it through the next. Okay? Okay moving on.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Brantley King</b> is a man who lives outside the law. Just coming out from his 3-years stint in prison, his best friend and partner in crime, Preppy throws him a homecoming party. However King is anything but in the celebratory mood, struggling to adjust after being thrown back into the outside world. He does however finds solace in inking tattoos. On the same night of his party where he caught the gaze of a pair of blue eyes observing him in a middle of one of his inking sessions, something powerful stirs within the darkness in him.<br><br><b>Doe</b> is a nobody, a girl who can't remember her name or her past memories. She's been living off the streets until she got picked up by a hooker named Nikki and took her in. They both ended up in the same homecoming party when Nikki convinced her that the only way to survive is to sell herself. A desperate act somehow led her into the confines of King and before she even realised what she had gotten herself into, she was about to become King's property.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433606587i/15119483.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>It shames me to say that I've not read anything by this author prior to this but when I saw that blurb, I just knew I had to read this one. So when I got a copy and went in with close to zero expectations, I sure as hell didn't expect to come out feeling like my brain has been blown into smithereens! I loved every single bit of the book- from the moment I picked it up till I put it down in an entire sitting, I was wailing in agony when it ended all too soon. <br><br>Both King and Doe were amazing as individuals but even more explosive when they came together. Equally they struggled with the attraction that had for each other; the lust and the confusion which brought out some well needed angst in the read. The author did an amazing job by creating these multi-layered characters and her portrayal of them will leave you feeling incredibly raw as you truly feel for these characters. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433608449i/15119879.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you love anti-heroes in your reads, then you'll enjoy King as much as I did. You'll first meet King as the scary and powerful alpha-male that you won't want to mess with, he's all kinds of dark and dangerous but you just can't stay away from him. But beneath that tough exterior is a man who is capable of great things and when the layers are slowly peeled off, it was just devastatingly beautiful to meet the real King. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I'd found myself again in the haunted eyes of a girl was just as lost as I was. Or maybe, we didn't find each other at all. Maybe, we just decided to be lost together."</i>
</blockquote><br>I really loved Doe as a heroine, she had a good amount of resilience albeit the vulnerability she possessed due to her memory loss. She was rather mouthy with King and didn't take any kind of bullshit from anyone, easily a feisty character with some spunk. But most of all, I loved that she had this internal struggle of not knowing who she really was. It really added on another dimension to her character that made me admired her even more. Can you imagine living in someone's body but not knowing or understanding that body at all? The portrayal of Doe being protective and not reckless of her ownself seriously garnered my respect for her character. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433606587i/15119484.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Above all, it was the fantastic mix of secondary characters that really brought this book to a complete winner for me. I cannot wait for you guys to meet Preppy, he was such a great addition to the read that made it light-hearted amidst the dark nature of the story. There's also Bear and Grace; together all these characters developed such a strong bond that the focal point of the story doesn't lie entirely with the MCs. It's crazy how I've grown such a strong attachment with them that had me crying and laughing throughout the read. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Although it's a relatively quick read, it sure packs one helluva punch. It's just one of those that you want to devour every single page slowly but yet you can't flip the pages fast enough to know what happens next. Even with a dreaded cliffhanger at the end, I had no complaints about this book at all. Every twist and turn was slotted in perfectly that was enough to blow my mind away. And thank God for the prologue teaser of the next book at the end to help tide the waiting!<br><br>It's dark, it's edgy, it will send you on an emotional rollercoaster that will enthralled you from start till the end; <u>King</u> is one masterpiece of a read that will knock the wind out of you when you're done. Undoubtedly another read that goes into my top reads of 2015, I definitely urge everyone to give this one a shot!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><u>King</u> is the first book in the King series. The second book, <u>Tyrant</u> will be out on August 17th.</i><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided by the author in exchange for an honest review.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433775460i/15140880.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/readingescapade" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

    <a title="Dee Montoya" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya"><img alt="Dee Montoya" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483914811p2/11880024.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/872186614?book_show_action=true">Mar 04, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dee Montoya" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dee Montoya" href="/user/show/11880024-dee-montoya">Dee Montoya</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=epic">epic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=hot-alpha-male">hot-alpha-male</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=h-o-t">h-o-t</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=kick-ass-awesome-heroine">kick-ass-awesome-heroine</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11880024-dee-montoya?shelf=my-fictional-boyfriends">my-fictional-boyfriends</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer872186614" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14683324678579204942"><b>******6+++++ Monumental Stars******</b><br/><br/><i>(ARC kindly provided by author)</i><br/><br/><br/>I keep typing and erasing words because is hard to describe the magnitude of my feelings for <i>King.</i> Everyday we waited for this highly anticipated novel was worth it, T.M Frazier's penmanship has deliver a smashing story that will rip your heart right out of your chest and play with every single one of your emotions. Be ready to cry, lust, love and hate <i>King.</i> This novel is definitely a top best of 2015 read. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/2013d5a6-c245-4604-a662-3b88a78717c3_zpsv76o9igh.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433521245i/15106527.jpg' alt=' photo 2013d5a6-c245-4604-a662-3b88a78717c3_zpsv76o9igh.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>King is a criminal,</span>
  <span id="freeText14683324678579204942" style="display:none"><b>******6+++++ Monumental Stars******</b><br><br><i>(ARC kindly provided by author)</i><br><br><br>I keep typing and erasing words because is hard to describe the magnitude of my feelings for <i>King.</i> Everyday we waited for this highly anticipated novel was worth it, T.M Frazier's penmanship has deliver a smashing story that will rip your heart right out of your chest and play with every single one of your emotions. Be ready to cry, lust, love and hate <i>King.</i> This novel is definitely a top best of 2015 read. <br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/2013d5a6-c245-4604-a662-3b88a78717c3_zpsv76o9igh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433521245i/15106527.jpg" alt=" photo 2013d5a6-c245-4604-a662-3b88a78717c3_zpsv76o9igh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>King is a criminal, a ruthless player of the lawless world he rules. The day he comes out of prison after serving three years for a crime that changed his life; he goes back into his world but nothing feels the same. He's feeling out of sorts and then he sees a pair of blue eyes so powerful that in an instant they ignite all the light and all the darkness that's inside of him.<br><br>Doe can't remember anything about her past, she's been living on the streets for the past two months but has no recollection of how she got there. Desperate for food and shelter she befriends a prostitute who has convinced her the only way to survived is to sell herself. Together they go to the homecoming party of the <i>King of the Causeway</i> looking for a way to carry their mission but the only thing they'll find is big troubles.<br><br>Doe can't believe her eyes when she sees the beautiful monster that she is sure will be her destruction or perhaps her salvation. King and Doe battle with the intensity of the hate and lust that is brewing between them. They are trapped in a dark world where lies and pain tie them together but why does the connection between them feels so good, so right?<br><br> <a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/25930508-1087-474f-922e-4237098dd03a_zpsxqljaijl.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433521246i/15106528.jpg" alt=" photo 25930508-1087-474f-922e-4237098dd03a_zpsxqljaijl.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The complexity of the characters in this story blew me away. King made me love him and hate him at the same time and Doe was simply the best. Her strength and resilience was both heartbreaking and inspiring. I can tell you that while reading this book I cried, laughed and felt every word so deeply that I seriously don't know what to do with myself now that I finished the book; thank God the second part <i>Tyrant</i> will be out soon.<br><br>This book ends on a cliffhanger and you know I'm highly allergic to those but the end of King didn't make me crazy, this story filled me up so much that is mostly excitement what I feel after reading it. When you read a book this magnificent you mostly feel appreciative and enamored with the creation of fiction. Don't miss out on this incredible story that will both brake you and make you. Amazing!!!!!!<br><br>My <i>King</i> music playlist:<br>*Closer by Nine Inch Nails<br>*Wrecking Ball by Jasmine Thompson <br>*Summertime Sadness by Lana Del Rey<br>*It Must Have Been Love by Kathleen Edwards<br><br><a href="http://s1366.photobucket.com/user/DVFmontoya/media/eedb3c60-9392-4c22-a823-0718ef73d9a9_zpsivuuh0rw.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1277732722" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1277732722" />
    <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts"><img alt="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1591195447p2/16496589.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1277732722?book_show_action=true">May 11, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts" href="/user/show/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts">Jx PinkLady Reviews ♡ @bookwormthoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16496589-jx-pinklady-reviews-bookwormthoughts?shelf=advance-copy">advance-copy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1277732722" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16631885905816162390">* <a href='http://amzn.to/1ALhF4i' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon US</a> * <a href='http://amzn.to/1AOJb0q' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon UK</a> *<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435178123i/15313921.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I love the premise of <b>KING.</b> There's a level of mystery running through that's highly intriguing. The early narrative had me wondering about the heroine's identity and other aspects of the story. I felt the promise of dark places that would stretch my comfort levels and emotions, some moments certainly did this but I really think the story could have pushed me further and taken more risks which would undoubtedly have raised my angst levels and garnered more emotion. <br/><br/>On th</span>
  <span id="freeText16631885905816162390" style="display:none">* <a href="http://amzn.to/1ALhF4i" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> * <a href="http://amzn.to/1AOJb0q" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a> *<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435178123i/15313921.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love the premise of <b>KING.</b> There's a level of mystery running through that's highly intriguing. The early narrative had me wondering about the heroine's identity and other aspects of the story. I felt the promise of dark places that would stretch my comfort levels and emotions, some moments certainly did this but I really think the story could have pushed me further and taken more risks which would undoubtedly have raised my angst levels and garnered more emotion. <br><br>On the surface King is the epitome of a bad boy who lives on the wrong side of the law. A career criminal, he thrives in the underground world taking what he wants and the women he lusts after. He successfully combines his endeavours with being a sought after tattoo artist, making him all the more sexy. <br><br>The heroine awakens to a blank past, her identity and memories washed away with whatever happened to her. This is the foundation for much of the intrigue element and kept me engaged in the story. I loved some of her quirkiness, her talking ten to the dozen and saying exactly what she thinks at often inappropriate times. This endeared me to her but, in stark contrast, there are moments I felt a lack of understanding for her character's thoughts and reasoning which slowly eroded my connection to the story as a whole. There are times that I felt frustrated with the direction of the story, the character development and the dialogue, especially relating to the heroine. <br><br>King's interaction with his close friends shows the light and shade of his character. There were times I loved his inner monologue and his attraction to the heroine, he made me smile and warmed my heart. Whilst I loved seeing the lighter side of his bad boy persona contrasting with his tough side, I wish king had shown me more of his dark side and that the contrast had been more shocking. I felt glimpses but I craved more and really felt the story could have taken me to darker places, given me more of an edge and thereby made the light feel so much more euphoric. This would have driven the angst levels higher and made my emotions soar. <br><br>Preppy, a secondary character completely stole the story, he was the highlight for me and I felt his character was the most developed within the context of the story. I especially loved the interaction between him and King, he literally lit up the pages with his dialogue and witty personality. <br><br><b>King </b>is overall an enjoyable read with some oh-my-goodness moments where my anticipation levels increased. I felt the story picked up pace and grit towards the end when I experienced a greater depth of emotion. Many of my reviewing friends rate this story a glorious 5 stars so I may be firmly in the minority on my individual thoughts, therefore if you love a bad boy hero who is really lovely on the inside than this story may be one you devour and enjoy. <br> <br><b>Excerpt</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br>“I hate the way you made me feel. Well, most of the time.” I spat. I was tired of dancing around the truth. “I hate the confusion you bring into my already confused life. I need this back and forth shit to end.” I took a deep breath. “I can’t take it anymore. You like me. You hate me. You like me. You want to kill me. You want to fuck me. You want me to stay. You want me to live. My head is fucking spinning over here.” My buzz faded faster than the setting sun. "You should leave. I don't want you here," I added.<br>"I know. I don't care." King said.<br>"Oh, I’m fully aware that you don’t care. That I know.”<br>"You don't know shit, Pup." King barked.<br>"Oh yeah? So you didn't just spend the entire night at the carnival all over me, saying sweet shit to me, making me feel like this stupid thing between us is something more than just a stupid thing, only to whip out your dick with someone else the very first chance you got? Go back to the fucking house, King. Go back to that girl. I hope she's everything you wanted.”<br>"I can't," King said evenly.<br>"Why not? Seemed easy for you before."<br>"Because, Pup, I can’t because I don't want to. No matter how hard I try to fight this, I'm drawn to you. You think I like this back and forth shit? You think you’re the only one who’s fucking confused here?" He shook his head like he couldn't believe the words that were coming out of his mouth. "I'm drawn to you," he repeated turning my chin up to him.<br>“What do you expect? Am I supposed to fall at your feet and thank you for being ‘drawn to me’?” Not only was he confusing, he was fucking infuriating. "Drawn to me? You're drawn to me! Well, let me just take off my fucking panties then, and let's do this shit. Yeah, you were really drawn to me. Tell me something, KING. Do most first dates end with the guy getting sucked off by another girl? I mean, I've never been on one, so you tell me. I could be wrong here. Because if the answer is yes, then this date has gone fucking swimmingly!"<br>"I'm...FUCK! “You think you know everything but you don’t. All you do is run those pretty lips of yours and expect me to be able to just give into you!” King threw his hands up in the air. “You make me fucking crazy, you know that!" he shouted.<br>"I make YOU crazy? How the fuck do you think I feel? Most of the time I don't know if you want to kill me or fuck me!" I screamed, every single word he spoke ignited my anger until it wasn’t something I could even begin to hold back.<br>King had the audacity to actually smile. He leaned forward and whispered seductively against my cheek, "Can't I want both, Pup?"<br>I pulled back and stood up.<br>"NO! You can't! And stop calling me, Pup. It's a stupid fucking name. I'm not your fucking pet!"<br>I paced the dock. My rage was at a boiling point I couldn't turn off. This was his fault. He’d made me into this lunatic.<br>King stood and grabbed my face with both hands, forcing me to look at him. "Yes you are," he said, as he lowered his lips and brushed them softly against mine in a move so gentle, so unlike him, it took me a few seconds before I registered what was happening.<br>Then, my anger returned, in full force. Using both my hands, I pushed against his chest until he had no choice but to release me.<br>"Fuck you! You don't want to keep me!" I shouted over my shoulder as I made my way to the front of the house and started down the gravel driveway. "Do you think I’m stupid? You wouldn't be getting your jollies while I'm in the next room if it was me you wanted."<br>A large hand grabbed my shoulder and spun me around.<br>"Let go of me!" I shouted.<br>"Listen, Pup. I’ve tried it your way. I tried gentle just now, but you didn't listen. Now, we're going to do it my way, and you're going to fucking listen. Don't make me have to cuff you again." He warned.<br>  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br>Advanced copy received from the author, via TRSoR, in exchange for my honest review thoughts.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Beverly" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly"><img alt="Beverly" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1466964369p2/13095060.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1301975340?book_show_action=true">Jun 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beverly" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beverly" href="/user/show/13095060-beverly">Beverly</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1301975340" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12111447843843218615">LIVE on AMAZON -> <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1JPyAFH'>http://amzn.to/1JPyAFH</a><br/><br/>Brantley <b>King</b> has just been released from prison and is at his welcome home party when he first meets Doe. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I didn’t know if I wanted to kill her or fuck her. Maybe both, but one thing was for sure. One way or another, I was going to make her scream. I was finally starting to feel like my old self again. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br/><br/>King isn’t your typical hero. He isn’t a knight in shining armor, a billionaire, or even a nice guy, but boy do I love this guy! King’s life w</span>
  <span id="freeText12111447843843218615" style="display:none">LIVE on AMAZON -&gt; <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1JPyAFH">http://amzn.to/1JPyAFH</a><br><br>Brantley <b>King</b> has just been released from prison and is at his welcome home party when he first meets Doe. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I didn’t know if I wanted to kill her or fuck her. Maybe both, but one thing was for sure. One way or another, I was going to make her scream. I was finally starting to feel like my old self again. </blockquote>
  </i>
</b> <br><br>King isn’t your typical hero. He isn’t a knight in shining armor, a billionaire, or even a nice guy, but boy do I love this guy! King’s life was never easy, but he is resourceful, resilient and a fighter. King isn’t easy to love at first, but the more you see of him and see what motivates him, he is hard not to love. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434340225i/15206869.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Doe is lost, barely holding on and completely hopeless. She was found left for dead in alley and while it is a miracle she is alive, she has no memory of who she is. Immediately, I was impressed with Doe, she is a survivor - a quality I love in a person. She is loving and compassionate, but incredibly strong and independent. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434340225i/15206870.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>When she first meets King she is starving to death and beyond desperate. Circumstances outside of her control, have put her on the wrong side of King - a place you don’t want to be. She has become indebted to him through these circumstances and from here the story really takes off. Doe has no choice, but to stay with King, he is the key to her survival. <br><br>This story took me by complete surprise. First, I loved seeing Doe and King struggle with their feelings. They are both lost and unsure, but their desire for each other is blatant. More so, I loved seeing the transformation and watching them open up with each other. I feel like both of these characters come with a U-Haul truck worth of baggage, but they see the value in each other.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434340225i/15206871.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>King delivers on so many elements. This is a darker novel, but it will take you on an emotional journey with heartbreak, surprise, and complete hotness. The ending left me gasping and begging for more. I wanted to shout from the rooftops for everyone to read it. Days later I still <b>need</b> everyone to read it. <b>I cannot recommend this book enough.</b><br><br><br><b>
  <i>ARC kindly provided in exchange for an honest review. </i>
</b><br><br>

<div id="review_897054278" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/897054278" />
    <a title="Flo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7643503-flo"><img alt="Flo" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597575025p2/7643503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/897054278?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Flo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Flo" href="/user/show/7643503-flo">Flo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=best-of-2015">best-of-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=dark-and-twisted">dark-and-twisted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7643503-flo?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer897054278" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16009692817726265637"><b>5 **<u>EPIC</u>** STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434446681i/15222476.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Oh, pup. How much fun this is going to be.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>How on earth do I even start writing this review? My feelings are so all over the place I don't know how to put them in order. I went through such a whirlwind of emotions - I cried, I was happy, I was frustrated, I was confused, I was scared, I was mad beyond measure and in the end I'm freaking frustrated and suspicious about what comes next. Something smells funny and I want to get to the bottom of it right now, but as it t</span>
  <span id="freeText16009692817726265637" style="display:none"><b>5 **<u>EPIC</u>** STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434446681i/15222476.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Oh, pup. How much fun this is going to be.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>How on earth do I even start writing this review? My feelings are so all over the place I don't know how to put them in order. I went through such a whirlwind of emotions - I cried, I was happy, I was frustrated, I was confused, I was scared, I was mad beyond measure and in the end I'm freaking frustrated and suspicious about what comes next. Something smells funny and I want to get to the bottom of it right now, but as it turns out we have to wait until August for the next book.<br><br>Oh well, enough time to tell you about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20611949-king" rel="nofollow noopener">King</a>. This is the first instalment in a two part series and also the first time I have read a book by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5769238.T_M_Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">T.M. Frazier</a> and certainly not the last. I guess by now you get that I really, really enjoyed this read. Let's talk story... <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Brantley King</b> is a criminal and a tattoo artist. Straight up, no bullshit, bad boy. He chose that kind of life a long time ago and never had plans to change his way of living. But ever since he got out of prison after a three year sentence he has had some issues adjusting to his old life. Booze, bras and blow have lost their appeal. And when a girl with big haunted eyes walks in on him screwing some faceless bimbo his world starts to tumble a little. <br><br><b>Doe</b>, as in Jane Doe, is a lost soul. She was found in the trash not too long ago, beaten up and with no memory about who she is or where she came from. No one is looking for her and the only way to survive on the streets is not the most appealing one at all.<br><br>Her desperation and search for protection leads her to a house party and what she finds there will either kill her or safe her life. Or maybe be a little of both...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434532685i/15233637.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To say these characters were interesting is the understatement of the century in my opinion. Every one in this book has so many layers and brings so many complications, undisclosed motives and unanswered questions to the table that my head was spinning to keep it all in check. <br><br>The first person I fell in love with was Samuel 'Preppy' Clearwater, King's geeky best friend with a little dark side. You can pretty much ask anyone who read this book and they will all tell you he is the person to meet in this universe. He makes you laugh the most and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[then he makes you cry even more. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The second person I was touched by was Doe. Imagine waking up and your whole life is gone. Anyone would break and give up. She is resilient and a survivor, but also way out of her depth. Not just because she doesn't know who she is or where the next meal will come from, but because she stumbles into a situation where she has to deal with the enigma that is King and his world is all kinds of dangerous.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I didn't know whether I wanted to kill her or fuck her.<br>Maybe both, but one thing was for sure.<br>One way or another, I was going to make her scream.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>King has a little hot and cold problem going on. Dangerous and highly possessive, but once he comes into contact with Doe he melts on sight. It's a constant battle between what he should do and what he wants to do. <br><br>I really appreciated the dual POV, seeing what goes on both in his head but also Doe's mind. None of the characters behave in a straight forward way. The circumstances are extraordinary and the reactions are erratic at times. King and Doe have an instant lust/hate/fear/curiosity attraction going on, but are too afraid or too calculated to act on them. <br><br>If you expect to read a straight up dark romance with a real bad boy you might be disappointed. In fact King is a rather good man, who just acts like the bad seed on the outside. He is capable to do atrocious things, but he has a really good heart hidden to all but a few, even if he doesn't want to admit it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434539102i/15234391.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“My life seems to be a bunch of questions piled on top of a bunch of questions, and frankly, I'm ready to add some fucking answers into the mix before my brain explodes and leaks out of my ears.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I found myself totally spellbound by this book. It was gritty, well written and littered with twists and turns. I hated putting it down and I didn't want it to end. The mysteries were driving me nuts and the cliffhanger was mean and yet very exciting. After three days I'm still stuck with it and I have so many conspiracy theories in my head it's likely to blow over any moment now.<br><br>I am tagging this book as a dark read, but it's not strictly that. There are some dark elements, but for the most part it's more of a mystery and suspense read. You just never get the complete picture and very little gets resolved by the end of this first instalment. In fact it gets more complicated and I was left with more questions than before.<br><br>The only saving grace for my sanity was my dear bestie, Supreet. The Buddy Read really helped me bouncing off ideas and theories as to what was going on. Thanks for the fabulous BR, my friend. &lt;33 Can't wait for <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25711641-tyrant" rel="nofollow noopener">Tyrant</a> to arrive. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598100i/14852514.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/flo_reads" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852521.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852522.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://plus.google.com/u/0/101016591301224002138" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431598236i/14852523.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/flocoffeeaddict/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431599699i/14852627.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_825218692" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/825218692" />
    <a title="S.M. West" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west"><img alt="S.M. West" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564323942p2/18424676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/825218692?book_show_action=true">Jan 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S.M. West" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S.M. West" href="/user/show/18424676-s-m-west">S.M. West</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook " href="/book/show/18758916-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=alpha">alpha</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=dark-read">dark-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18424676-s-m-west?shelf=broken">broken</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer825218692" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer404989653976960906"><b>3.5 STARS</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/KING2_zpsfogb1ymm.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434720552i/15255974._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo KING2_zpsfogb1ymm.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I've been seriously hankering for this book for soooo long and perhaps my expectations were too high…<br/><a href='http://imgur.com/TXshuS9' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434720552ra/15255975.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I know I'm in the minority here. King is definitely an anti-hero, he’s hateful, vengeful, dangerous and volatile. I'll admit, I usually fall instantly for an alpha asshole jerk but for some reason, this didn't happen with King and I really wanted it to. <br/><br/><a href='http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/KING_zpsgqzn7up7.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434720552i/15255976._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo KING_zpsgqzn7up7.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Doe, a homeless and starving young woman with amnesia, is in a living hell and stumbles into King's life. King claims her as</span>
  <span id="freeText404989653976960906" style="display:none"><b>3.5 STARS</b><br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/KING2_zpsfogb1ymm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434720552i/15255974._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo KING2_zpsfogb1ymm.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I've been seriously hankering for this book for soooo long and perhaps my expectations were too high…<br><a href="http://imgur.com/TXshuS9" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434720552ra/15255975.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know I'm in the minority here. King is definitely an anti-hero, he’s hateful, vengeful, dangerous and volatile. I'll admit, I usually fall instantly for an alpha asshole jerk but for some reason, this didn't happen with King and I really wanted it to. <br><br><a href="http://s1292.photobucket.com/user/swidso/media/KING_zpsgqzn7up7.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434720552i/15255976._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo KING_zpsgqzn7up7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Doe, a homeless and starving young woman with amnesia, is in a living hell and stumbles into King's life. King claims her as his as payment for something that was stolen from him. I liked Doe although I thought she was too nice and forgiving at times. She had this innocence about her that came across easily.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/pP8Rkkf" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434720552ra/15255977.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Her relationship with King is one emotional roller coaster. Like I said, I struggled A LOT because his emotions gave me whiplash. Poor Doe had no clue if he was coming or going, if he'd be in a rage or somewhat normal. There was a moment when I was almost on Team King, I was beginning to feel something positive, maybe even warm and fuzzy while he was on his date with Doe...<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/y4419v4" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422047144ra/13449398.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Then, I was completely thrown for a loop, which seriously had me spitting nails with the shit he pulled afterwards...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/ig1Adlz" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434720725ra/15256013.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It came totally from left field. I would have perhaps understood if something triggered his colossal dick move or something. <br> <br>King and Doe's physical relationship was also volatile - <b>“I’d never both hated and wanted something so much in my entire life.”</b><br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/id2t6am" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434720552ra/15255978.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This is my first T.M. Frazier book but it won’t be my last. While I wanted to like this more, it was still a quick and entertaining read and there were some characters that stole the story, if you ask me. I found myself loving both Preppy and Bear, King's BFFs. And I never realized just how much I adored Preppy until tragedy hits...<br><a href="http://imgur.com/tGZV1EE" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434720552ra/15255979.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Overall, the story felt rushed at times, and while I don’t need to dwell on things or be labour the point, it just seemed like areas that could have been further explored or explained were just skimmed over. For instance, there is one horrific incident with Doe and it just felt like drama for drama's sake. There was no fallout or discussions about it afterwards, when the nightmare she experienced could have been explored a bit more. <br><br>The ending has a real good cliffy and an unexpected twist.<br><a href="http://imgur.com/QKqTMtc" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1434720725ra/15256014.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I also really liked the sneak peek into the prologue of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25711641.Tyrant__King___2_" title="Tyrant (King, #2) by T.M. Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">Tyrant</a>. I will be reading it. I do want to know how this all unfolds.<br><br><b>For more reviews and blog posts.</b><br> <a href="http://slutsistas.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1417650623i/12469037._SX540_.png" height="90" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="404989653976960906" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1296501891" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1296501891" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515708587p2/10367112.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1296501891?book_show_action=true">Jun 01, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/10367112-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=cliff-hanger">cliff-hanger</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=dark">dark</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=loved-it">loved-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=abuse">abuse</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=gritty">gritty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10367112-michelle?shelf=2015">2015</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1296501891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18302192203278032088"><i>ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review. </i><br/><br/><br/>Holy Shit... <b>KING</b> by T.M. Frazier was a F*CKING BRILLIANT EPIC READ!!!! Pardon my language, but this book was just everything I expected and so much more. It was raw, dark, sensual, captivating, gritty, and an emotional journey that had all the FEELS. This book will grip you to the core and leave you begging for more of KING and his intense personality!!<br/><br/><a href='https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/18308213279' title='#King_Frazier by ms.meesh, on Flickr' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433523041i/15106875._SX540_.jpg' width='640' height='400' alt='#King_Frazier' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>T.M. Frazier's writing was intoxicating, spellbinding, and hypnotic that you couldn</span>
  <span id="freeText18302192203278032088" style="display:none"><i>ARC provided by author in exchange for an honest review. </i><br><br><br>Holy Shit... <b>KING</b> by T.M. Frazier was a F*CKING BRILLIANT EPIC READ!!!! Pardon my language, but this book was just everything I expected and so much more. It was raw, dark, sensual, captivating, gritty, and an emotional journey that had all the FEELS. This book will grip you to the core and leave you begging for more of KING and his intense personality!!<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/18308213279" title="#King_Frazier by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433523041i/15106875._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="400" alt="#King_Frazier" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>T.M. Frazier's writing was intoxicating, spellbinding, and hypnotic that you couldn't put this book down. It is one of the reads that you had to devour but at the same time savor. The writing and storytelling was just so gripping that Ms. Frazier literally played and toyed with every emotions. She was like a puppet master who had our emotions on strings. And when you thought you were finally getting to that part of the story where you could feel at ease, Ms. Frazier just had to rip and gut your heart out. Yes, it's one of those reads that plucked, pulled, and toyed with every range of emotions. You wanted to shout, cry, hate, love, and scream WHY KING WHY!! I must be a glutton for punishment because I LOVED EVERY SINGLE MOMENT of this emotional, dark, gritty, cruel and raw read.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/17889576703" title="#king1 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433561467i/15113513._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="421" alt="#king1" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>If you are looking for a book hero that will open up doors and whisper sweet nothings in your ear, then I'm sorry to disappoint you because <i>KING</i> is none of that. But if you are looking for a hero who acts on his emotions, a total bad ass alpha male hero, a ruthless killer, and who doesn't take shit from no one, then look no further than KING. King, is a ruthless criminal who recently just got of prison serving for a crime that changed his outlook and purpose in life. There are three things that matters to King... Max, Preppy, and Doe.<br><br>Doe is a homeless young girl who has no recollection of her past hence the name "Doe". When she finds herself at one King's house party, she didn't expect a circumstance of events would leave her in bed with a monster. King makes it known she belongs to him. His possession. His to take. Simply, his. But through time her perception of him changes. The man she sees as the devil and monster soon transforms into a man that she needs, wants and craves. A man who gives Doe a reason to be alive.<br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/18343845570" title="#King2 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433613868i/15120839._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="491" alt="#King2" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The relationship of Doe and King is not a kind of relationship that can be described as simple. It is one that is complicated but a tangible bond that can't be described by words alone. It's a bond that is deep, raw, heartfelt, palpable, and gritty. It is the kind of love that can destroy you but at the same time give you a meaning to fight and live for. So with no recollection of her past, Doe leans on King and submits to him fully. The walls that surrounds King's heart are crumbling because Doe is the only one who can make him FALL. She gives him hope. His light in the darkness. But what happens when the truth is finally revealed of Doe's identity, can she truly belong to him? <br><br><a href="https://www.flickr.com/photos/66034700@N08/18344650118" title="#KING3 by ms.meesh, on Flickr" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433615633i/15121248._SX540_.jpg" width="640" height="429" alt="#KING3" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>In all honesty, this book is one of those reads that is on my list of favorite reads of 2015. A book of this magnitude really showcases how resilient, raw, captivating, spell-binding and bewitching Doe, King, Preppy and Bear are in this book. What I love about this story is how T.M. Frazier can grip us with her masterful storytelling. She makes you FEEL and EXPERIENCE every heartbreak, anger, lust, hatred, and sorrow of all her characters. When a book can leave you breathless and in awe, then you know you have read an amazing book. And that was what KING was for me. Ms. Frazier did a phenomenal job interweaving so many raw elements but at the same time gave us a story with so much depth, honesty, grit, and palpable emotions. She was able to elevate this story to another level where you saw that looks can be deceiving and not to judge a character by their appearance. I want to thank Ms. Frazier for introducing readers to a complicated and complex hero that has stole my heart. So if you are looking for a book where you are taken down a dark, raw journey that has possibility of a luminous and hopeful ending then I HIGHLY RECOMMEND you to read KING. <br><br><br><a href="http://s848.photobucket.com/user/msmeesh983/media/b373ddc87926837ffa753458fb29e1_zpsdn2eln3k.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1445639384i/16683506.gif" alt=" photo b373ddc87926837ffa753458fb29e1_zpsdn2eln3k.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Review can also be found on Four Chicks Flipping Pages: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly.com">http://fourchicksflippingpages.weebly...</a> </i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/5769238.T_M__Frazier" title="T.M. Frazier" rel="nofollow noopener">T.M. Frazier</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18302192203278032088" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="Judith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/29540292-judith"><img alt="Judith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421966041p2/29540292.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/912571792?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Judith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Judith" href="/user/show/29540292-judith">Judith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/20611949-king">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer912571792" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10807678761403309691"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>They call me Doe<br/>As in Jane Doe</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434483496i/15228442._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Doe is living on the streets,not knowing her name or anything about her background due to memory loss.She is befriended by a girl called Nikki who tells her the best she can hope for is to get close to a Biker who can shelter her and protect her.She knows what this means but sees no other option than agreeing to go to a party at King's house....<br/><br/><b>KING</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434489067i/15229228._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><b>DOE</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434483496i/15228444._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>King has just been released from prison and his friend Preppy is throwing him a welcome home party.While</span>
  <span id="freeText10807678761403309691" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>They call me Doe<br>As in Jane Doe</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434483496i/15228442._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Doe is living on the streets,not knowing her name or anything about her background due to memory loss.She is befriended by a girl called Nikki who tells her the best she can hope for is to get close to a Biker who can shelter her and protect her.She knows what this means but sees no other option than agreeing to go to a party at King's house....<br><br><b>KING</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434489067i/15229228._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b>DOE</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434483496i/15228444._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>King has just been released from prison and his friend Preppy is throwing him a welcome home party.While at the party Nikki makes a huge mistake and King decides Doe must re pay the debt by staying with him.She does make an escape only to be brought back by King.At this point,all is not what it seems though...<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>So I did something.Something that made the decision to go after her an easy one.A decision that would forever change the lives of everyone around me.<br>Some for the good.<br>Some for the bad.<br>Some for the dead.<br>I found out who Doe really was.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>King is a complex character...Scary,fierce,a typical Alpha Male but deep down he had a softer side and a strong loyalty to those he cared about.What started of as one thing with Doe turned into something else along the way...<br>Doe,had a kind of innocence about her but also a fiesty spirit as she battled with the girl she was now and the one she left behind<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1434484636i/15228582._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first half of the book IMO was about character development and it's not until the second half when things really start to happen.There are two great secondary characters in Bear and Preppy....oh Preppy what's not to love about him.He and King have been friends since a young age and have a strong friendship.The Author created such a brilliant,unique character in him..I just ADORED him...everyone should have a Preppy in their lives!!<br><br>There's been a lot said in reviews about the ending and my God the last 15% of this book was amazing.Something happened and I thought no the Author's not going there....and yes she totally did and I was .......well I'm not saying anything to spoil this.<br>Secrets are revealed and there's something that I totally wasn't expecting...<br>Brilliant,loved it...August can't come soon enough!!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10807678761403309691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
